This ensures that any exception raised within a middleware is converted to an appropriate HTTP response before propagating to the next middleware, preventing middleware from receiving exceptions.\\n\\n## Comparison to WSGI Middleware\\n\\nUnlike traditional WSGI middleware which implements the full callable protocol directly, Django's middleware using MiddlewareMixin (django/utils/deprecation.py, lines 275-331) uses the factory pattern. The factory takes get_response as an argument in __init__(), and the instance is callable via __call__(). This allows Django to:\\n1. Build the middleware stack at initialization time (one-time operation)\\n2. Ensure symmetric request/response processing (onion model)\\n3. Short-circuit unnecessary middleware execution\\n4. Handle exceptions within the middleware chain cleanly\\n5.
